[12/26/2024 6:43 PM] blue_laser_02
I'm thinking of having the Anime Top 10's on Saturday so make sure to get any last minute anime watched (at least partially). 
I would recommend trying to have at least one seasonal anime for each season (winter, spring, summer, fall). If you're unsure what anime you've seen fall under which season use this website https://www.livechart.me/winter-2024/tv , this website shows every anime that aired for each season in 2024. Make sure to check it out to see if you have seen a show from a certain season, or if you don't have any anime from a season and want to find a quick one to check out before the top 10's
